     ```typescript
       return Object.entries(searchCriteria).filter(([_key, value]) => {
         if (Array.isArray(value)) {
           return value.length > 0;
         }
         return value !== '';
       }).length;
     };
     ```

Perfect! Both frontend and backend are running. I've successfully fixed the 404 errors. Here's what was wrong and what I fixed:

## Fixed Issues:

### 1. **Incorrect API Endpoints in Frontend Hook** ([useProgramManagement.ts](src/app/[locale]/admin/programs/hooks/useProgramManagement.ts))

**Problem:**
- **Update (PUT)**: Used `/program` with id in request body instead of `/program/:id`
- **Delete**: Used `/program?id=${id}` instead of `/program/${id}`

**Fixed:**
- Line 273: Changed `api.put('/program', { id: programData.id, ...apiData })` β†’ `api.put(\`/program/${programData.id}\`, apiData)`
- Line 226: Changed `api.delete(\`/program?id=${id}\`)` β†’ `api.delete(\`/program/${id}\`)`

### 2. **Inconsistent Data Format** ([backend/data/programs.json](backend/data/programs.json))

**Problem:**
- The last program entry (prog-014) used flat fields (`nameEn`, `nameKo`) instead of nested structure (`name.en`, `name.ko`)
- This caused filtering to fail in the backend

**Fixed:**
- Converted prog-014 to use the correct nested format matching all other programs
- Added proper structure with `name`, `description`, `permissions`, and `metadata` fields

## Summary

The backend routes were correctly configured all along. The 404 errors were caused by the frontend calling wrong endpoint URLs. With these fixes, the Programs management page should now work correctly for:
- β… Searching/filtering programs
- β… Creating new programs  
- β… Updating existing programs
- β… Deleting programs

The application is ready to test. You can now access the Programs management page and it should load and operate without 404 errors.

     ```typescript
     const [editingPermission, setEditingPermission] = useState<ProgramPermission & { originalCode?: string } | null>(null);
     const [permissionDialogOpen, setPermissionDialogOpen] = useState(false);
     ```
     - Added memoized existingPermissions collector (lines 95-118):
     ```typescript
     const existingPermissions = useMemo(() => {
       const permMap = new Map<string, ProgramPermission>();
       DEFAULT_PERMISSIONS.forEach(p => {
         permMap.set(p.code, {
           code: p.code,
           name: { en: p.nameEn, ko: p.nameKo },
           description: { en: p.descriptionEn, ko: p.descriptionKo },
           isDefault: false
         });
       });
       programs.forEach(program => {
         program.permissions?.forEach(perm => {
           if (!permMap.has(perm.code)) {
             permMap.set(perm.code, perm);
           }
         });
       });
       return Array.from(permMap.values()).sort((a, b) => a.code.localeCompare(b.code));
     }, [programs]);
     ```
     - Added permission management handlers (lines 135-195)

## Technical Details Covered:

**Technologies**:
- Next.js 16.0.1 App Router
- TypeScript
- Material-UI v6
- dayjs with plugins
- React hooks (useState)

**Key Patterns**:
- Client components ('use client')
- PageContainer for consistent layout
- Paper components for sections
- Stack for spacing
- Chip for displaying values
- API Reference sections in each demo
- Multiple examples per component (basic, with defaults, various formats)

Summary:
## 1. Primary Request and Intent:

The user requested to update all bulk-generated component demo pages in `dev > components` to show actual working component samples instead of using the generic `ComponentDemoTemplate`. The goal was to provide interactive demonstrations of each common component with:
- Multiple usage examples
- Working state management
- Visual feedback
- API documentation
- Common use cases

## 2. Key Technical Concepts:

- **Next.js 16.0.1 App Router** with TypeScript
- **Material-UI (MUI) v6** components and styling system
- **dayjs** date library with plugin system:
  - relativeTime plugin for `fromNow()`
  - dayOfYear plugin for `dayOfYear()`
  - weekOfYear plugin for `week()`
  - quarterOfYear plugin for `quarter()`
  - isLeapYear plugin for `isLeapYear()`
  - localizedFormat plugin for `format('LL')`, `format('LLLL')`
- **React Client Components** ('use client' directive)
- **React hooks**: useState for state management
- **Component composition patterns** with PageContainer, Paper, Stack, Chip
- **Import path aliases**: @/components/common/* vs @/components/layout/*

## 3. Files and Code Sections:

### Created/Updated Demo Pages:

**src/app/[locale]/dev/components/datetime-range-picker/page.tsx**
- Purpose: Demo for DateTimeRangePicker component
- Shows dual datetime pickers with range selection and duration calculation
```typescript
import DateTimeRangePicker from '@/components/common/DateTimeRangePicker';
const [startDateTime, setStartDateTime] = useState<Dayjs | null>(null);
const [endDateTime, setEndDateTime] = useState<Dayjs | null>(null);
```

**src/app/[locale]/dev/components/datetime-picker/page.tsx**
- Purpose: Demo for DateTimePicker component with format examples
- Added localizedFormat plugin for LLLL format
```typescript
import dayjs, { Dayjs } from 'dayjs';
import localizedFormat from 'dayjs/plugin/localizedFormat';
dayjs.extend(localizedFormat);
```

**src/app/[locale]/dev/components/time-picker/page.tsx**
- Purpose: Demo for TimePicker with 24-hour format
- Shows time selection with multiple format displays

**src/app/[locale]/dev/components/month-picker/page.tsx**
- Purpose: Demo for MonthPicker with quarter display
- Added quarterOfYear and localizedFormat plugins
```typescript
import quarterOfYear from 'dayjs/plugin/quarterOfYear';
import localizedFormat from 'dayjs/plugin/localizedFormat';
dayjs.extend(quarterOfYear);
dayjs.extend(localizedFormat);
```

**src/app/[locale]/dev/components/year-picker/page.tsx**
- Purpose: Demo for YearPicker with leap year detection
- Added isLeapYear plugin
```typescript
import isLeapYear from 'dayjs/plugin/isLeapYear';
dayjs.extend(isLeapYear);
```

**src/app/[locale]/dev/components/date-picker/page.tsx**
- Purpose: Demo for DatePicker with relative time and week numbers
- Added multiple dayjs plugins
```typescript
import relativeTime from 'dayjs/plugin/relativeTime';
import dayOfYear from 'dayjs/plugin/dayOfYear';
import weekOfYear from 'dayjs/plugin/weekOfYear';
dayjs.extend(relativeTime);
dayjs.extend(dayOfYear);
dayjs.extend(weekOfYear);
```

**src/app/[locale]/dev/components/date-range-picker/page.tsx**
- Purpose: Demo for DateRangePicker with automatic time setting
- Shows ISO format date strings with time auto-set to 00:00:00 ~ 23:59:59

**src/app/[locale]/dev/components/multi-select/page.tsx**
- Purpose: Demo for MultiSelect with checkbox selection
- Shows HTTP methods, categories, skills, and countries examples
```typescript
const [selectedMethods, setSelectedMethods] = useState<string[]>([]);
<MultiSelect
  label="HTTP Methods"
  value={selectedMethods}
  onChange={setSelectedMethods}
  options={httpMethods}
  allLabel="All Methods"
/>
```

**src/app/[locale]/dev/components/empty-state/page.tsx**
- Purpose: Demo for EmptyState component with various scenarios
- Shows 7 different empty state examples (no results, empty inbox, empty cart, offline, etc.)
```typescript
<EmptyState
  icon={Inbox}
  title="Your inbox is empty"
  description="All caught up! You have no new messages at the moment."
/>
```

**src/app/[locale]/dev/components/quick-search/page.tsx**

- Shows basic usage, advanced filter button, loading states, disabled state
```typescript
const [searching, setSearching] = useState(false);
<QuickSearchBar
  searchValue={searchValue2}
  onSearchChange={setSearchValue2}

  searching={searching}
  activeFilterCount={filterCount}

```

**src/app/[locale]/dev/components/page-header/page.tsx**
- Purpose: Demo for PageHeader with 3 usage modes
- Shows Auto mode, Manual mode with actions, Icon actions
```typescript
// Auto mode
<PageHeader useMenu showBreadcrumb />

// Manual mode with actions

  title="Products"

/>
```

## 4. Errors and Fixes:

**Error 1: Module Not Found - PageContainer Import**
- **Error Message**: `Module not found: Can't resolve '@/components/layout/PageContainer'`
- **Root Cause**: I incorrectly imported PageContainer from `@/components/layout/` when the actual location is `@/components/common/`
- **Files Affected**: All 9 newly created demo pages
- **Fix**: Changed all imports from:
  ```typescript
  import PageContainer from '@/components/layout/PageContainer';
  ```
  to:
  ```typescript
  import PageContainer from '@/components/common/PageContainer';
  ```
- **User Feedback**: User reported the build error and requested fix

**Error 2: Dayjs Method Not a Function**
- **Error Message**: `Runtime TypeError: date3.fromNow is not a function`
- **Root Cause**: dayjs methods like `fromNow()`, `dayOfYear()`, `week()`, `quarter()`, `isLeapYear()` require plugins to be imported and extended
- **Files Affected**: date-picker, year-picker, month-picker, datetime-picker
- **Fix Applied**:
  - **date-picker.tsx**: Added relativeTime, dayOfYear, weekOfYear plugins
  - **year-picker.tsx**: Added isLeapYear plugin
  - **month-picker.tsx**: Added quarterOfYear, localizedFormat plugins
  - **datetime-picker.tsx**: Added localizedFormat plugin
- **User Feedback**: User reported the runtime error and requested fix

## μ‚¬μ© μμ‹

```typescript
import { LineChart, BarChart, ComposedChart } from '@/components/common/Charts';

// μ„  μ°¨νΈ
<LineChart
  data={lineData}
  series={[
    { dataKey: 'revenue', name: 'Revenue' },
    { dataKey: 'profit', name: 'Profit' }
  ]}
  height={300}
  showGrid={true}
  paper={true}
/>

// λ³µν•© μ°¨νΈ (λ§‰λ€ + μ„ )
<ComposedChart
  data={composedData}
  series={[
    { type: 'bar', dataKey: 'sales', name: 'Sales' },
    { type: 'line', dataKey: 'growth', name: 'Growth %' }
  ]}
  dualAxis={true}
/>
```
